# Quest Hub Expansion — DepthPack MEGA

700 grounded quests (QST-026 → QST-725).

## QST-026 — A Bell Without a Rope (Frostbriar)
- **Giver:** Caravan Guard
- **Type:** Collect
- **Objectives:**
  1. Collect **Silt-grit Plank** (ID 31370).
  2. Collect **Worn Liniment** (ID 32765) *or* substitute from the same subcategory.
  3. Return and pick a payoff.
- **Rewards:**
  - **River-smooth Cap** (ID 32199) *or* **Mire-touched Memo** (ID 31665)
  - coin, rep, and a rumor unlock.
- **Follow-ups:**
  - after 3 completions, unlocks a named NPC contract.

## QST-027 — A Favor Paid in Wax (Glimmerdeep)
- **Giver:** Waykeeper
- **Type:** Bargain for
- **Objectives:**
  1. Bargain for **Silt-grit Chew** (ID 31047).
  2. Bargain for **Windworn Charm** (ID 30378) *or* substitute from the same subcategory.
  3. Return and pick a payoff.
- **Rewards:**
  - **Harbor-wet Cap** (ID 31003) *or* **Pine-sap Page** (ID 31213)
  - coin, rep, and a rumor unlock.
- **Follow-ups:**
  - after 3 completions, unlocks a named NPC contract.
